var is_jump_col = 0;
function chbCot_Change() {
if (document.getElementById('chbCot').checked) {
Cookies.set('is_jump_col', 1, { expires: 7 });
is_jump_col = 1;
} else {
Cookies.set('is_jump_col', 0, { expires: 7 });
is_jump_col = 0;
}
// alert(is_jump_col);
}
function chbDong_Change() {
if (document.getElementById('chbDong').checked) {
Cookies.set('is_jump_col', 0, { expires: 7 });
is_jump_col = 0;
} else {
Cookies.set('is_jump_col', 1, { expires: 7 });
is_jump_col = 1;
}
// alert(is_jump_col);
}
var isthb, istrcn, iskhac;
isthb = 0;
istrcn = 0;
iskhac = 0;
var containerK = $("#qi-menu-danh-muc-khac");
var containertcn = $("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh");
$(document).ready(function () {
$(".qi-div-item-TCN").click(function () {
rurl = $(this).attr('rurl');
window.location.href = rurl;
});
$(".bt-mo").attr('title', 'Ẩn/hiện khối lọc.');
$(".bt-zoom").attr('title', 'Xem toàn màn hình.');
$(".bt-config-cot").attr('title', 'Cấu hình hiển thị cột dữ liệu.');
$(document).mouseup(function (e) {
// Danh mục khác
if (!containerK.is(e.target)
&& containerK.has(e.target).length === 0) {
iskhac = 0;
$("#qi-menu-danh-muc-khac").hide();
}
// truy cập nhanh
if (!containertcn.is(e.target)
&& containertcn.has(e.target).length === 0) {
istrcn = 0;
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh").hide();
$("#qi-image-thong-bao-child").hide();
}
});
$("#qi-image-danh-muc-khac").click(function () {
try {
if (iskhac === 0) {
$("#qi-menu-danh-muc-khac").show();
} else {
$("#qi-menu-danh-muc-khac").hide();
}
iskhac = 1 - iskhac;
istrcn = 0;
isthb = 0;
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh").hide();
$("#qi-menu-thong-bao").hide();
$("#qi-image-thong-bao-child").hide();
} catch (err) {
console.log(err);
}
});
$("#qi-image-thong-bao").click(function () {
try {
$("#qi-image-thong-bao-child").show();
} catch (err) {
//console.log(err);
}
});
$("#qi-image-truy-cap-nhanh").click(function () {
try {
if (istrcn === 0) {
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh").show();
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh ul").html("");
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh ul").addClass("loading");
$.ajax({
url: 'https://truong.hanoi.edu.vn/DanhSachTruyCapNhanh.aspx',
}).done(function (msg) {
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh ul").removeClass("loading");
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh ul").html(msg);
});
} else {
$("#qi-menu-truy-cap-nhanh").hide();
}
istrcn = 1 - istrcn;
iskhac = 0;
isthb = 0;
$("#qi-menu-danh-muc-khac").hide();
$("#qi-menu-thong-bao").hide();
$("#qi-image-thong-bao-child").hide();
} catch (err) {
// console.log(err);
}
});
});
function goThongBaoHeThong() {
document.location.href = 'https://truong.hanoi.edu.vn/DSThongBaoHeThong.aspx';
}
function goHomeLogo() {
document.location.href = 'https://truong.hanoi.edu.vn/Default.aspx';
}
function goHuongDan() {
var url = 'http://huongdan.csdl.moet.gov.vn';
window.open(url);
}
function goHuongDanUrl(url) {
window.open(url);
}
function goHoTro() {
window.open(url);
}
function cbSoftwareShowImage(image) {
var input2 = document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl04_cbSoftware_Input");
var input = document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl03_cbSoftware_Input");
if (input) {
input.style.background = "url(https://truong.hanoi.edu.vn/images/iconPM/" + image + ".jpg) no-repeat";
}
if (input2) {
input2.style.background = "url(https://truong.hanoi.edu.vn/images/iconPM/" + image + ".jpg) no-repeat";
}
}
toastr.options.closeButton = true;
toastr.options.positionClass = "toast-bottom-right";
function notification(type, message) {
if (type == 'success') {
toastr.success(message, '<i>Thành công</i>');
} else if (type == 'error') {
toastr.error(message, '<b>Lỗi</b>');
} else if (type == 'warning') {
toastr.warning(message, '<b>Cảnh báo</b>');
} else {
toastr.info(message, 'Thông báo');
}
}

<script type="text/javascript">
function RadWindowprompt_detectenter(id, ev, input) {
if (!ev) ev = window.event;
if (ev.keyCode == 13) {
var but = input.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("button")[0];
if (but) {
if (but.click) {
but.click();
}
else if (but.onclick) {
but.focus();
var click = but.onclick;
but.onclick = null;
if (click) click.call(but);
}
}
return false;
}
else return true;
}
</script>

function RadWindowManager1_OnClientClose(sender, args) {
var ajaxManager = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ctl00_RadAjaxManager1").ajaxRequest("RadWindowManager1_Close");
var arg = args.get_argument();
if (arg != null) {
refreshGrid();
notification('success', arg);
}
}
function openRadWinHoSo(url) {
var viewportwidth;
var viewportheight;
if (typeof window.innerWidth != 'undefined') {
viewportwidth = window.innerWidth,
viewportheight = window.innerHeight;
} else if (typeof document.documentElement != 'undefined' && typeof document.documentElement.clientWidth != 'undefined' && document.documentElement.clientWidth != 0) {
viewportwidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth, viewportheight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
} else {
viewportwidth = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientWidth,
viewportheight = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientHeight;
}
if (viewportwidth > 1280)
viewportwidth = viewportwidth - 100;
radopen(url, "RadWindow1", viewportwidth, viewportheight - 50);
}
function refreshGrid() {
var masterTable = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ctl00_RadGrid1").get_masterTableView();
masterTable.rebind();
}
var grid;
function pageLoad() {
grid = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ctl00_RadGrid1");
setBorderRowGrid(grid, 5);
checkValidYear();
}
var isTrangThaiChange = false;
var isTrangThaiOpen = false;
function OnClientItemCheckedTrangthai(sender, eventArgs) {
isTrangThaiChange = true;
}
function OnClientDropdownCheckedAllTrangthai(sender, eventArgs) {
isTrangThaiChange = true;
}
function OnClientDropdownOpenTrangthai(sender, eventArgs) {
isTrangThaiOpen = true;
}
function OnClientDropdownCloseTrangthai(sender, eventArgs) {
if (isTrangThaiOpen == true && isTrangThaiChange == true) {
////firing postback
//console.log('fired');
refreshGrid();
}
isTrangThaiOpen = false;
isTrangThaiChange = false;
}
function checkValidYear() {
var masterTable = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ctl00_RadGrid1").get_masterTableView();
var count = masterTable.get_dataItems().length;
var item;
for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
item = masterTable.getCellByColumnUniqueName(masterTable.get_dataItems()[i], "NGAY_SINH");
var item_val = item.innerHTML;
if (item_val != '') {
var year = item_val.split('/')[2];
if ((year < 1980) || (year > (new Date()).getFullYear())) {
item.classList.add("invalid-value");
item.setAttribute("title", "Giá trị không hợp lệ");
}
}
}
}
function openWinContentTemplate() {
var radwindow = $find('ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ctl00_rwdShowColumn');
radwindow.show();
}
function CheckMaxItemViewRadgrid(sender, args) {
var maxNumberOfItems = 20000;
var dest = args.get_destinationListBox();
var totalCount = dest.get_items().get_count();
var itemsToTransferCount = args.get_items().length;
if (totalCount >= maxNumberOfItems) {
args.set_cancel(true);
notification('error', "Bạn chỉ được chọn hiển thị tối đa 20000 cột.");
} else if (totalCount + itemsToTransferCount > maxNumberOfItems) {
while (totalCount + itemsToTransferCount > maxNumberOfItems) {
itemsToTransferCount--;
args.get_items().pop();
}
}
}
function responseEnd(sender, eventArgs) {
SetGridHeight();
ResizeInUserControl();
RepaintGrid();
}
$(document).ready(function () {
SetGridHeight();
ResizeInUserControl();
RepaintGrid();
});

GetStep2Data();
}

function GetStep2Data() {
var step = $("#hdStep").val();
if (step == "2") {
setTimeout(function () {
var masterTable = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_ctl00_RadGrid1").get_masterTableView();
masterTable.rebind();
}, 15000);
//step2Runer = setTimeout(GetStep2Data, 10000);
}
else {
clearTimeout(step2Runer);
}
}

if (confirm("Bạn có muốn thực hiện thao tác này?")) {
return true;
}
else {
return false;
}
}
